data-interchange="[https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1517162024945-595ae6bca1a4.jpg, small],  [https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1517162024945-595ae6bca1a4.jpg, large]" /></div></div></div><div class="main-container"><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x grid-margin-y"><div class="cell medium-12 large-8"><article id="post-21875" class="post-21875 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-agile-testing tag-agile-testing"><header><h1 class="entry-title">Agile Testing vs. Waterfall Testing</h1> <time class="updated" datetime="2019-03-25T08:45:18+01:00">Posted on March 25, 2019 at 8:45 am.</time><p class="byline author">Written by <a href="https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/members/nicolag/profile/" rel="author" class="fn">Nicola</a></p></header><div class="entry-content"> <span class="rt-reading-time" style="display: block;"><span class="rt-label rt-prefix">Reading Time: </span> <span class="rt-time">3</span> <span class="rt-label rt-postfix">minutes</span></span><p>When it comes to testing any software project, there is a dilemma of choosing the approach that fits the task best. Agile and Waterfall are two diverse testing strategies that are currently most popular. Learn how to tell between the two and choose what works best for you from this post. Check out our list of advantages and disadvantages for every approach as well.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><h3 style="text-align: center;">What is Agile Testing?</h3><p>Agile testing is a software testing methodology that matches the postulates of Agile software development. Agile implicates that the requirements of the client and the development team develop gradually. In this approach, the development and testing processes are aligned with the demands of the customer.</p><h5>Benefits of Agile Testing</h5><ul><li><strong>Minimal planning</strong> required due to the simple structure.</li><li><strong>Little documentation</strong>.</li><li>Testers work <strong>jointly with developers</strong> on the project.</li><li>Best<strong> fit for small projects</strong>. It also <strong>works fine for long-term</strong></li><li><strong>Bugs don’t pile up</strong>. It takes place simultaneously with the project development.</li><li><strong>Quick issue solving</strong>. There is a separate testing place for every iteration.</li><li><strong>Continuous feedback</strong>. The Team and the Product Owner are always on the same page about the project development and quality assurance.</li><li><strong>Test-driven development</strong>. When using Agile, testing is performed during implementation.</li><li><strong>Flexible </strong>and supports changes.</li></ul><h5>Shortcomings of Agile Testing:</h5><ul><li><strong>Requires </strong>continuous efficient <strong>communication </strong>between testers and developers.</li><li><strong>Blurred </strong>organizational <strong>structure</strong>.</li><li>Only senior programmers can make<strong> crucial decisions during team meetings</strong>.</li></ul><h2></h2><h2><noscript><img class="wp-image-21846 aligncenter" src="https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_1024/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-1024x682.jpg" alt="software testing news" width="500" height="333" srcset="https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_1024/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-1024x682.jpg 1024w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_300/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-300x200.jpg 300w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_768/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-768x512.jpg 768w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_544/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-544x362.jpg 544w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_135/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-135x90.jpg 135w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_225/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-225x150.jpg 225w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_1051/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974.jpg 1051w" sizes="(max-width: 639px) 98vw, (max-width: 1199px) 64vw, 500px" /></noscript><img class="lazyload wp-image-21846 aligncenter" src='https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_lqip,ret_wait,w_500,h_333/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-1024x682.jpg' data-src="https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_1024/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-1024x682.jpg" alt="software testing news" width="500" height="333" data-srcset="https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_1024/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-1024x682.jpg 1024w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_300/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-300x200.jpg 300w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_768/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-768x512.jpg 768w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_544/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-544x362.jpg 544w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_135/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-135x90.jpg 135w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_225/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974-225x150.jpg 225w, https://cdn.shortpixel.ai/client/q_glossy,ret_img,w_1051/https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/photo-1544256718-3bcf237f3974.jpg 1051w" data-sizes="(max-width: 639px) 98vw, (max-width: 1199px) 64vw, 500px" /></h2><h3 style="text-align: center;">What is Waterfall Testing?</h3><p><strong><em>Waterfall testing is a software testing methodology that matches the postulates of Waterfall software development.</em></strong> Waterfall implicates that there is a sequence of stages in which the output of each stage becomes the input for the next. Waterfall approach is also known as the linear-sequential life cycle model.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>As you can probably already tell, Agile testing is applied together with the Agile development approach. Consequently, Waterfall testing is applied in the scope of the Waterfall development.</p><h5>Advantages of Waterfall Testing</h5><ul><li><strong>Well-structured</strong> and <strong>well-documented</strong> testing process.</li><li><strong>Fits projects of any complexity</strong>.</li><li><strong>All the features</strong> of the project are <strong>developed and delivered together</strong>.</li><li>Testers and developers do not need to communicate continuously. They <strong>work independently</strong>.</li><li><strong>Easy to manage</strong>. With Waterfall, every stage has its deliverables and a strict review method.</li><li><strong>Easy to adapt</strong> in case a team changes or different teams work in shifts.</li></ul><h5>Drawbacks of Waterfall Testing</h5><ul><li>It requires <strong>excessive documentation</strong>.</li><li><strong>Strict structure</strong>.</li><li><strong>Not perfect for large</strong>-scale <strong>projects</strong>.</li><li>Testing takes part only <strong>at the end of the project</strong> In some cases, bugs are easier solved before they pile up.</li><li>In case the<strong> client requirements are not precise</strong> from the start, it is <strong>less effective</strong> compared to Agile.</li></ul><h2></h2><h3 style="text-align: center;">How to Choose Between Agile and Waterfall Testing?</h3><p>As you can see, both Waterfall and Agile have their advantages when it comes to project quality testing. Yet, every method has its limitations. To pick the right approach for your project, you need to consider what aspects of each method are more crucial for you.</p><p>We believe that <a href="https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/8-key-points-of-agile-testing-marketing-management/">Agile testing</a> is more flexible, motivating, and result-oriented. In real life, project requirements are hardly ever concise, clear and unchangeable all the time from the very beginning till the very end of the project development. Choosing Agile, you will be able to align testing with programming and make sure your customer gets exactly what they need and when they need it.</p><h3 style="text-align: center;">Final Thoughts</h3><p>Agile and Waterfall are two of the most popular approaches to development and quality testing. Yet, they are quite different when it comes to structure and implementation. It’s important to choose the approach that corresponds to your needs best and stick with it carefully.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><p>We believe that Agile is the only way to go in the conditions of ever changing client demands and startup pivots. This flexible and simple approach is a safe choice for any project.</p><p>&nbsp;</p><hr /><p><strong>About the Author</strong></p><p>Maria Redka is a Technology Writer at <a href="https://mlsdev.com/">MLSDev</a>. It is web and mobile app development company in Ukraine. Our focus area includes a full range of services in mobile and web app development as well as design, consulting and testing.</p><div class="post-views post-21875 entry-meta"> <span class="post-views-icon dashicons dashicons-chart-bar"></span> <span class="post-views-label">Post Views: </span> <span class="post-views-count">827</span></div></div><footer class="panel clearfix"><h4>Tags:</h4> <a href="/?tag=agile-testing" class="button">Agile Testing</a></footer></article><div class="post_nav"><nav class="navigation post-navigation" role="navigation" aria-label="Posts"><h2 class="screen-reader-text">Post navigation</h2><div class="nav-links"><div class="nav-previous"><a href="https://huddle.eurostarsoftwaretesting.com/ransomware-and-cybersecurity/" rel="prev">How Safe Are You?
